균열

속성

설명

**깊이**

균열의 깊이를 제어합니다.

**길이**

균열의 길이를 조정합니다.

**너비(Width)**

균열의 너비를 조정합니다.

**수축**

균열의 끝을 수축시켜 더 뾰족한 결과를 만듭니다.

**부드러움**

균열의 수직 가장자리를 부드럽게 합니다.

균열 외부에 노이즈를 추가합니다.

**작은 강도**

**큰 강도**

큰 UV 스케일 노이즈 왜곡을 형태에 적용합니다.

**노이즈 스케일**

노이즈의 스케일을 제어합니다.

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/ko/reference/terrain/shape-layers/landscape#undefined-71)

화산

속성

설명

**분화구 감쇠**

# Hole Layers | World Creator

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/hole-layers#overview)

Overview


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Hole Layers enable you to add holes for caves or other structures that should pierce through the landscape by either painting directly in World Creator or importing a bitmap from an external source.

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/hole-layers#results)

Results


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.world-creator.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2837684122-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FM6zsxw2jbMYEZbKqEwpa%252Fuploads%252Fdcm7FLGeWDDxZXDxQYz2%252Freference_holelayer_02.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De08ba572-f422-447e-a316-e7b0404ced54&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=10d765d8&sv=2)

Putting a cave entry in a mountain

![](https://docs.world-creator.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2837684122-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FM6zsxw2jbMYEZbKqEwpa%252Fuploads%252FNMqU7asrN0aQFkqjqPaO%252Fscreenshot_0.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5aee62a7-11ab-446b-a71d-438ab8db7c63&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=eda89be1&sv=2)

Full terrain with the cave

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/hole-layers#layer-parameters)

Layer Parameters


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/hole-layers#mask-layer-settings)

Mask Layer Settings

![](https://docs.world-creator.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2837684122-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FM6zsxw2jbMYEZbKqEwpa%252Fuploads%252FC0SGwEwhI71J98Ombn4Z%252Freference_masklayers_01.webp%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd0831440-5af4-46ca-9f8b-d06b9827c230&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=19d2cbc6&sv=2)

*   **Show Mask** Shows the mask on the terrain.
    
*   **Import/Export** Allows you to import or export the mask.
    
*   **Edit** Allows you to edit the mask using brushes.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/hole-layers#area-settings)

Area Settings

The Area Settings allow you to freely position Hole Layers on your terrain and offer simple controls to blend them into your terrain.

![](https://docs.world-creator.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2837684122-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FM6zsxw2jbMYEZbKqEwpa%252Fuploads%252FwICbEjd9Ic6RRA6HFeGW%252Freference_shapelayers_information_03.webp%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D574b2b9b-1ac6-4222-8815-05cf481415b7&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=12f61cd8&sv=2)

*   **X/Y** The position of the area on the terrain.
    
*   **Area Scale** The size of the area.
    
*   **Rotation** The rotation of the area
    
*   **Fit to Terrain** Matches the area to the terrains full size.
    
*   **Blending** Controls the opacity of the whole shape layer.
    
*   **Blend Size** Adds a fade in to the area.
    
*   **Blend Roundness** Rounds the corners of the face.
    

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/hole-layers#editing-parameters)

Editing Parameters


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

These parameters are only available when the hole layer is in **Edit** mode.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/hole-layers#brush-tools)

Brush Tools

Simple paint tools to modify the hole. Choose your preferred tool by clicking on it, and then draw with your mouse (press the left mouse button on the terrain). The following functions are available:

*   **Paint** Adds to the mask.
    

*   **Erase** Removes from the mask.
    

*   **Smooth** Averages the mask under the brush.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/hole-layers#actions)

Actions

The operations are utilized to rapidly implement precise modifications. Please refer to the list below to understand the function of each operation.

*   **Flip X** Flips the mask along the X axis.
    

*   **Flip Y** Flips the mask along the Y axis.
    

*   **Rot Left** Rotates the mask by 90°.
    

*   **Rot Right** Rotates the terrain by 90°.
    

*   **Clear** Sets the whole mask to 0.
    

*   **Fill** Sets the whole mask to 1.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/hole-layers#brush-settings)

Brush Settings

Properties

Description

**Brush**

Allows you to specify several preinstalled brushes as well as import your own custom brushes.

**Falloff Mode**

Offers different brush falloff modes.

**Brush Radius**

The radius of the brush.

**Brush Smooth**

The size of the brush smoothing.

**Brush Strength**

Controls the strength of the current selected brush.

**Rotation**

Rotates the brush pattern.

**Random Rotation**

Adds random rotation to the brush pattern.

**Align to Draw Direction**

Orients the brush pattern to the drawing direction.

Last updated 2 months ago

*   [Results](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/hole-layers#results)
    
*   [Layer Parameters](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/hole-layers#layer-parameters)
    
*   [Mask Layer Settings](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/hole-layers#mask-layer-settings)
    
*   [Area Settings](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/hole-layers#area-settings)

*   [Brush Tools](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/hole-layers#brush-tools)

# Mask Layers | World Creator

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/mask-layers#overview)

Overview


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Mask Layers enable you to mask out specific sections of your terrain by painting directly in World Creator or importing a bitmap from an external source. Mask Layers are compatible with the distribution system and can thus be referenced by filters and materials.

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/mask-layers#video-guide)

Video Guide


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

World Creator Guide

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/mask-layers#results)

Results


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.world-creator.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2837684122-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FM6zsxw2jbMYEZbKqEwpa%252Fuploads%252F4zAZXzwvfjyg2QN9AT9u%252Fwalkthrough_masks_03.webp%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D513929c7-b957-4773-bd5b-0b205788c112&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d251eaeb&sv=2)

Creating a mask

![](https://docs.world-creator.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2837684122-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FM6zsxw2jbMYEZbKqEwpa%252Fuploads%252F0HYvvcMmwLqLknoZI9W0%252Fwalkthrough_masks_05.webp%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2e35221f-6da9-4b1b-a957-1e722000ca11&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5bd81132&sv=2)

# Bridge Tools | World Creator

The World Creator Bridge simplifies importing terrains from World Creator to your preferred rendering application for processing and editing.

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/export/bridge-tools#supported-applications)

**Supported Applications**


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Detailed descriptions and usage guides for each bridge can be found in their respective sub-article. Currently, the use of bridges is supported by the following applications

*   [Unreal Engine](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/export/bridge-tools/unreal-bridge)
    
*   Unity Engine
    
*   [Blender](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/export/bridge-tools/blender-bridge)
    
*   [Cinema 4D](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/export/bridge-tools/cinema-4d-bridge)
    
*   [Houdini](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/export/bridge-tools/houdini-bridge)
    

circle-info

If you cannot find your preferred Digital Content Creation (DCC) or workflow, please contact our support team or leave a message on the Discord server. If there is enough demand, we will check what is needed to implement it.

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/export/bridge-tools#bridge-usage-instructions)

**Bridge usage instructions**


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Bridge allows you to import terrain seamlessly by clicking two buttons. To start, load your terrain from World Creator. Then click on the sync button in the application bar at the top of the main panel.

![](https://docs.world-creator.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2837684122-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FM6zsxw2jbMYEZbKqEwpa%252Fuploads%252FltxogoR5CG2iyBoLB6iK%252Fwalkthrough_bridge_export_01.webp%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc52e9fb0-8e44-415d-baf6-72d93d59604c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4716f443&sv=2)

Location of the Sync Button

Upon pressing the button, World Creator automatically exports the necessary files to recreate the scene within another application.

To complete the syncing process, click the Synchronize button in the user interface of the bridge for your respective program. The bridge loads all relevant maps and sets up the terrain for your 3D scene based on the parameters selected within the bridge interface. (Refer to the documentation for installation instructions specific to your bridge).

![](https://docs.world-creator.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2837684122-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FM6zsxw2jbMYEZbKqEwpa%252Fuploads%252Fp5ByUd7eA9mh88e2FZcc%252Fwalkthrough_bridge_export_02.webp%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D232245de-0157-4ef9-8e3f-dc65224709c3&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1402b780&sv=2)

The World Creator Bridge interface in Cinema 4D

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/export/bridge-tools#internal-functionality-of-the-bridge-including-diy-guide)

**Internal Functionality of the Bridge (Including DIY Guide)**


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you wish to create a custom version of the bridge, either for a different/custom DCC or with additional functionality specific to your workflow, you will find all relevant information about the bridge's internal processes here.

When you click the sync button in World Creator, all relevant information and maps are exported to the Sync directory. This directory is located by default at "_\[User\]_\\Documents\\World Creator\\Sync\\". Here you will find the following files:

*   **XML Info (bridge.xml)**
    
    Contains relevant terrain information such as resolution, size, minimum and maximum height, number of tiles, as well as details about splat layers.
    

*   **Height map (heightmap\_x\_y.raw)**
    
    The heightmap is available in raw uint16 format. If you are unable to load raw format and have access to Python, you may try using Pillow. This conversion tool is used by Blender, C4D, and Houdini.
    

*   **Color map (colormap\_x\_y.png)**
    
    The colormap stores the color multiplication values of World Creator and the gradients of the materials.
    

*   **Texture map (texturemap\_x\_y.png)**
    
    This map is similar to the colormap, but it also includes all texture and material information. In essence, this is a complete precomputed colormap of the terrain.
    

*   **Splat map (splatmap\_x\_y.tga)**
    
    Contains the splat layers. Depending on the number of layers, it contains a maximum of 4 layers, which are stored in the order R->A. The number and names of the splat layers can be found in the bridge.xml file.
    

*   **Assets**
    
    All assets referenced in the scene are stored here. The names are the same as in the bridge.xml file.
    

All the bridges do from here is convert the information into a usable scene asset in each program and offer some additional options (e.g. different renderers, material setups).

Last updated 1 year ago

Was this helpful?

*   [Supported Applications](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/export/bridge-tools#supported-applications)
    
*   [Bridge usage instructions](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/export/bridge-tools#bridge-usage-instructions)
    
*   [Internal Functionality of the Bridge (Including DIY Guide)](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/export/bridge-tools#internal-functionality-of-the-bridge-including-diy-guide)
    

Was this helpful?

# 노이즈 제거 | World Creator

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/ko/reference/terrain/effects/denoise#undefined)

개요


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Denoise 효과는 분포에서 소규모 노이즈를 제거합니다.

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/ko/reference/terrain/effects/denoise#undefined-1)

매개변수


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

속성

설명

**편차**

탐지 알고리즘의 강도를 변경합니다.

**임계값**

탐지 알고리즘의 임계값을 변경합니다. 값이 높을수록 저주파 노이즈를 더 많이 걸러냅니다.

**반경**

노이즈 제거 블러의 강도입니다.

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/ko/reference/terrain/effects/denoise#undefined-2)

결과


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

# Sand | World Creator

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/simulation-layers/sand#overview)

Overview


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Sand Simulation adds granular sediment to the terrain. The Simulation moves the material from an unstable position downhill until a stable angle is reached and in the process fills up crevices and cracks.

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/simulation-layers/sand#video-guide)

Video Guide


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

World Creator Guide

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/simulation-layers/sand#parameters)

Parameters


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Properties

Description

**Slope Angle**

The angle at which sediment will no longer continue moving. The talus formed at the bottom of a mountain will take on this angle.

**Erosion Angle**

The angle at which sediment will become unstable and start slipping downhill.

**Spawn Level**

In which level the sediment gets added to the terrain.

**Spawn Amount**

The amount of sediment added to the terrain.

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/simulation-layers/sand#results)

Results


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.world-creator.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2837684122-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FM6zsxw2jbMYEZbKqEwpa%252Fuploads%252Fta1qFO8hYua7OrGdFg5V%252Fwalkthrough_simulations_sand_01.webp%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7bece237-3330-4284-a794-85dc9c11bb8c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d1058320&sv=2)

sand simulation

![](https://docs.world-creator.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2837684122-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FM6zsxw2jbMYEZbKqEwpa%252Fuploads%252FLDgEC7palpgRhQD7NO5Z%252Fwalkthrough_simulations_sand_02.webp%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5f18afa3-1119-4b0c-ab6a-c3bb5bf40ef9&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f2d85713&sv=2)

sand simulation painted on the terrain

Last updated 6 months ago

# Unreal Bridge | World Creator

The World Creator Bridge for Unreal Engine allows you to seamlessly import your terrain creations into Unreal Engine for use in your game projects. For version 2.0 of the bridge we have completely overhauled everything about the bridge. It now comes with support for object import using PCG and an auto terrain setup that finds the ideal settings depending on the size of the terrain you want to sync.

circle-exclamation

We recommend a max pixel resolution of 16x16k. 32x32k should also work, above that we haven't tested and is really not recommended in terms of performance.

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/export/bridge-tools/unreal-bridge#installation)

**Installation**


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Close Unreal Engine if it's open.
    
*   Go to your Unreal project folder and create a folder called **Plugins** in your project root (if you don't have one already).
    
*   Copy the **WorldCreatorBridge** folder from the unzipped bridge file into the **Plugins** folder.
    

The Bridge dialog is located under **Window -> World Creator Bridge**.

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/export/bridge-tools/unreal-bridge#parameters)

**Parameters**


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/export/bridge-tools/unreal-bridge#xml)

XML

In this section you can link your synced terrain. Once you have selected a bridge file press the **Read XML Data** button to auto import the ideal settings.

circle-info

Before any operation in the bridge make sure to press the **Read XML Data** button since that data is required for both the landscape and object import.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/export/bridge-tools/unreal-bridge#import-parameters)

Import Parameters

*   **Asset Name**
    
    Specify the prefix of the terrain gameobject in the level.
    

*   **Import Materials**
    
    If this value is True, the bridge imports materials from World Creator. Set this to False if you only want to import the landscape and do everything regarding the material. Keep in mind that if Import Layers is enabled you will still get the material layers as landscape layers on your landscape.
    

*   **Import Layers**
    
    When enabled, the bridge will import individual material layers from World Creator as landscape layers and with a blending landscape material. If disabled a single Texturemap will be used for the whole terrain.
    

*   **Reset Terrain on Resync**
    
    Deletes and recreates the terrain on resync. Disable this if you just changed your heights and want to keep existing **Edit Layers** through the sync.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/export/bridge-tools/unreal-bridge#landscape-parameters)

Landscape Parameters

*   **Section Size**
    
    The number of quads in a single section (UE landscape parameter).
    

*   **Sections per Component**
    
    The number of sections in a single component (UE landscape parameter).
    

*   **Landscape Scale**
    
    The scale of the landscape, this influences the landscape and the objects that are imported using the bridge.
    

*   **World Partition**
    
    Enables World Partition for the landscape.
    

*   **Grid Size**
    
    Number of components per landscape streaming proxies per area (UE WP parameter).
    

*   **World Scale**
    
    Number of components per landscape world partition region per axis (UE WP parameter).
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/export/bridge-tools/unreal-bridge#objects)

Objects

*   **Reimport Objects**
    
    Reimports all imported objects on sync. Disable this to keep modifications made to your auto imported sync objects.
    

*   **Reset Placement**
    
    Clears all placement in the scene. Recreates the pcg for detail/instance meshes, refreshes the pointclouds and cleans the detail landscape layer maps used to paint dense objects onto the terrain.
    

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/export/bridge-tools/unreal-bridge#workflow-example)

**Workflow Example**


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

# Fluid | World Creator

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/simulation-layers/fluid#overview)

Overview


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Fluid Simulation Layer executes a fluid simulation on your terrain, which can be everything from really fast flowing water to more viscose substances like lava.

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/simulation-layers/fluid#video-guide)

Video Guide


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

World Creator Guide

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/simulation-layers/fluid#parameters)

Parameters


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Properties

Description

**Viscosity**

The viscosity of the fluid controls how fast and fluid the matter reacts. This allows you to change the appearance of your fluid from water to a thicker substance like lava.

**Speed**

The speed at which the liquid travels over the terrain.

**Wind Direction**

Controls the direction of the additional wind force.

**Wind Direction**

Controls the direction of the additional wind force.

**Wind Strength**

Adds an additional wind force to the velocity of the simulated matter.

**Wind Level Multiplier**

Links the wind strength to the current level step. This is helpful because the distance between pixels increases with each level step and the effect needs to be scaled with that in mind.

**Wind Randomness**

Randomizes the wind direction, allowing for a more natural result.

**Spawn Level**

In which level the sediment gets added to the terrain.

**Spawn Amount**

The amount of sediment added to the terrain.

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/simulation-layers/fluid#results)

Results


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.world-creator.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2837684122-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FM6zsxw2jbMYEZbKqEwpa%252Fuploads%252FWO7lcS32RptC7r9wyUKf%252Fwalkthrough_simulations_fluid_01.webp%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3e2f2d1e-5be1-4224-adc8-dae24b08f951&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1d499c4&sv=2)

![](https://docs.world-creator.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2837684122-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FM6zsxw2jbMYEZbKqEwpa%252Fuploads%252FmO5JE9VZgaAwYEZfVVgm%252Fwalkthrough_simulations_fluid_02.webp%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df12451e3-c7ad-4fc0-8dea-8f5b09a771f0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ab93527a&sv=2)

# Houdini Bridge | World Creator

The Houdini World Creator Bridge enables you to import your terrain creations seamlessly into Houdini, either as a Houdini heightfield for further processing or as a displaced grid for rendering.

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/export/bridge-tools/houdini-bridge#installation)

**Installation**


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Launch Houdini and navigate to the Assets menu to open the Install Asset Library panel. Here, locate the .hdanc file you extracted from the downloaded bridge file.

circle-info

Ensure that you are using a Python3-based Houdini installation. The default build type for Houdini 19.0 and above should be this.

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/export/bridge-tools/houdini-bridge#parameters)

**Parameters**


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **XML File**
    
    Locate the .xml file for the desired sync project. For WC 22 and above, this file is located by default at _**\[User\]**_**\\Documents\\World Creator\\Sync\\**
    

*   **World Scale**
    
    Sets the scale factor for the terrain.
    

*   **Height Scale**
    
    Set the scale factor for the terrain's height.
    

*   **Output Type**
    
    Choose the output type between heightfield for processing or displaced grid for rendering.
    

*   **Import Splat Layers to Heightfield**
    
    Imports the splat layers from your World Creator materials as individual heightfield layers which can be helpful if you want them as masks for further processing in Houdini (only available for heightfields).
    

*   **Material**
    
    Specify the renderer for which the materials need to be created.
    

*   **Import Material Layers**
    
    Switch between using individual terrain layers or a baked color map in the generated material.
    

*   **Reset Materials**
    
    Allows you to protect any changes made to specific material layers from the synchronization process. Note that this only works if you keep the original names!
    

*   **Force UV Scaling**
    
    This scales the UVs of the grid slightly so that all height map wrapping artifacts should be invisible. This is applied to all octane terrains by default since it has a bug that prevents wrapping from being disabled.
    

circle-info

The **wc\_bridge** node must always be unlocked to function properly. This is because it internally creates material nodes in a matnet which can be generated only when it is unlocked.

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/export/bridge-tools/houdini-bridge#workflow-example)

**Workflow Example**


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This example demonstrates how to render a terrain in Houdini using Octane. The Canyon sample file provided with World Creator will be used. The same steps can be applied to any other World Creator project.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/export/bridge-tools/houdini-bridge#sync-from-world-creator)

**Sync from World Creator**

Select the Synchronise button in the application bar located at the top of the main panel to export all relevant data from World Creator automatically.

![](https://docs.world-creator.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2837684122-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FM6zsxw2jbMYEZbKqEwpa%252Fuploads%252FUvwccwFp3frQSR6fSBf8%252Fwalkthrough_bridge_terrain.webp%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df208acd0-1a26-4e20-9532-4c722bc60871&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d3923a4f&sv=2)

_The World Creator scene before the sync_

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/export/bridge-tools/houdini-bridge#sync-into-houdini)

**Sync into Houdini**

Create a **WC Bridge** node within a geometry network. To enable Octane, set the **Output Type** to **Grid** and the **Material** to **Octane**, and click the Synchronize button.

![](https://docs.world-creator.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2837684122-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FM6zsxw2jbMYEZbKqEwpa%252Fuploads%252F21ZB4vDWNfxOxqLWpeJI%252Fwalkthrough_bridge_houdini_01.webp%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D806cf4b9-2d28-42de-a36f-7b68f4d4af58&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cb85261&sv=2)

_Synced terrain in Houdini_

Since we had Import Layers activated we now have individual submaterials for all material layers from World Creator, which can be further modified inside Houdini.

circle-info

Note that the Octane bridge supports a maximum of 12 layers.

Let's give our terrain a winter look by changing the top sediment layer to snow to make it more visually appealing. To achieve this, obtain the **Sediment** diffuse material and insert a **Tool\_MixTexture** node between the color map and the output, with white Color RGB as the color. Undoubtedly, creating the snow effect in World Creator could lead to a more precise outcome, but for the purpose of this guide, we will use Houdini.

![](https://docs.world-creator.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2837684122-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FM6zsxw2jbMYEZbKqEwpa%252Fuploads%252Fvhny2tFGJ2ywyvnGUDUz%252Fwalkthrough_bridge_houdini_02.webp%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D63b668d7-edd3-4f59-914b-00b1fcfaf845&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6e98984b&sv=2)

_Synced terrain with altered splat maps in Houdini_

The landscape should resemble this now.

Using the bridge offers the significant advantage of faster iteration between World Creator and Houdini. To demonstrate this, set the seed of the entire terrain within World Creator to 1 in order to create a distinct scene that conforms to our original terrain design.

In order to maintain the snow cover changes in our Houdini material, disable the **Reset Materials** parameters in the bridge parameters. The bridge subsequently scans the terrain materials for pre-existing layers, retaining any modifications made to them while reloading any pertinent new textures. The sole prerequisite for this to function correctly is that you preserve the original names of the diffuse materials.

Although we are currently using this feature for a relatively simple modification, it can be used with more complex materials such as tri-planar shaders while maintaining the same iteration speed between World Creator and Houdini.

![](https://docs.world-creator.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2837684122-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FM6zsxw2jbMYEZbKqEwpa%252Fuploads%252FaST9q1b2Vb3wEu9Eu7Yl%252Fwalkthrough_bridge_houdini_03.webp%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da45bff52-1935-411b-b091-421e5f168de0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=459da4ce&sv=2)

_Material changes applied to a freshly imported terrain with a different seed_

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/export/bridge-tools/houdini-bridge#sync-into-houdini-heightfield)

**Sync into Houdini - Heightfield**

In addition to importing our World Creator terrain as a regular mesh for rendering, we can also import it as a heightfield. To do this, modify the **Output Type** to **Heightfield** and optionally enable Import Splat Layers to Heightfield.

This will allow us to load individual materials from World Creator as heightfield layers for use in simulations.

![](https://docs.world-creator.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2837684122-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FM6zsxw2jbMYEZbKqEwpa%252Fuploads%252FQX1CHu7tmZPGUkkLTpuA%252Fwalkthrough_bridge_houdini_04.webp%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D963d02f4-0b84-4664-b0f4-abbaedc297f8&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=db1d533b&sv=2)

_The terrain imported into Houdini as a heightfield with its splat layers as heightfield layers_

Last updated 1 year ago

Was this helpful?

*   [Installation](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/export/bridge-tools/houdini-bridge#installation)
    
*   [Parameters](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/export/bridge-tools/houdini-bridge#parameters)
    
*   [Workflow Example](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/export/bridge-tools/houdini-bridge#workflow-example)
    
*   [Sync from World Creator](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/export/bridge-tools/houdini-bridge#sync-from-world-creator)
    
*   [Sync into Houdini](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/export/bridge-tools/houdini-bridge#sync-into-houdini)
    
*   [Sync into Houdini - Heightfield](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/export/bridge-tools/houdini-bridge#sync-into-houdini-heightfield)

# Unity Bridge | World Creator

The World Creator Bridge for Unity enables you to effortlessly import your terrain creations into Unity for use in your game projects.

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/export/bridge-tools/unity-bridge#installation)

**Installation**


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Open Unity and import the .unitypackage found in the downloaded bridge file either by using the Assets/Import Package/Custom Package... menu or by dragging and dropping it into the Project view in Unity.

To access the Bridge dialog, navigate to Window/World Creator Bridge.

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/export/bridge-tools/unity-bridge#parameters)

**Parameters**


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **Select Bridge .xml File**
    
    Locate the .xml file for the desired sync project. For WC 22 and above, this file is located by default at _\[User\]_\\Documents\\World Creator\\Sync\\
    

*   **Terrain Asset Name**
    
    Specify the prefix for all terrain gameobjects created by the bridge.
    

*   **Delete unused Assets**
    
    Unused assets are automatically removed upon synchronization.
    

*   **Import Layers**
    
    Toggle between using individual terrain layers or a baked color map in the generated materials.
    

*   **Split Threshold**
    
    Sets the grid size of the terrain tiles in Unity. Increasing the split threshold reduces the number of tiles.
    

*   **World Scale**
    
    Specifies the scaling factor for the terrain.
    

*   **Material Type**
    
    Choose the rendering pipeline of your Unity project or utilize a custom material.
    

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/export/bridge-tools/unity-bridge#workflow-example)

**Workflow Example**


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

In this example, we will transfer our terrain into Unity. The Canyon sample file that comes with World Creator will be used. These steps can be applied to any other World Creator project.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/export/bridge-tools/unity-bridge#sync-from-world-creator)

**Sync from World Creator**

Click the sync button in the application bar at the top of the main panel to export all necessary data from World Creator automatically.

![](https://docs.world-creator.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2837684122-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FM6zsxw2jbMYEZbKqEwpa%252Fuploads%252FUvwccwFp3frQSR6fSBf8%252Fwalkthrough_bridge_terrain.webp%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df208acd0-1a26-4e20-9532-4c722bc60871&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d3923a4f&sv=2)

_The World Creator scene before the sync_

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/export/bridge-tools/unity-bridge#sync-into-unity)

**Sync into Unity**

Under **Window/World Creator Bridge**, open the Bridge dialog window.

Choose the appropriate **Material Type** based on your project's render pipeline. For our case, as we are using the Built-In RP, we need to configure it to **Standard**.

Once you press the **Synchronize** button, the terrain will be loaded into the scene.

![](https://docs.world-creator.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2837684122-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FM6zsxw2jbMYEZbKqEwpa%252Fuploads%252F5Uz5ZjX1GgQFhGdWotyp%252Fwalkthrough_bridge_unity_01.webp%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4380200a-b324-4fb3-b895-d42f4ffb0733&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f0041d25&sv=2)

_Synced terrain in Unity_

Last updated 5 months ago

# Cinema 4D Bridge | World Creator

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/export/bridge-tools/cinema-4d-bridge#installation)

**Installation**


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy the **wc\_bridge** folder found in the downloaded bridge file, and paste it into the 'plugins' folder of your Cinema 4D installation.

To launch the bridge interface in Cinema, go to the **Extensions** menu and select **World Creator Bridge**.

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/export/bridge-tools/cinema-4d-bridge#parameters)

**Parameters**


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **XML File**
    
    Locate the .xml file for the sync project you wish to use. By default, for WC 22 and above, it is located in \[SYSTEM DRIVE\]:\\User\\Documents\\World Creator\\Sync\\
    

*   **Obj Name**
    
    Specify the prefix for all terrain objects created by the bridge. Modify this setting if you want to import a second terrain, otherwise, the old one will be replaced.
    

*   **World Scale**
    
    Specifies the scale factor for the terrain.
    

*   **Height Scale**
    
    Specifies the scale factor for the height of the terrain.
    

*   **Subd Viewport/Render**
    
    Specifies the amount of terrain subdivision.
    

*   **Octane Texture Displacement**
    
    Enabling this option adds a second plane to the scene that utilizes Octane's Voxel Displacement to render the terrain. A terrain with a displace modifier that is disabled for rendering will still be present in the scene to enable the scattering of meshes.
    

*   **Import Layers**
    
    Toggle between using individual terrain layers or a baked color map in the generated material.
    

*   **Adjust Clipping**
    
    This option automatically adjusts the clipping distance of the viewport camera so that the entire terrain becomes visible. (This only modifies the viewport camera, not the one used for rendering!)
    

*   **Reset Objects**
    
    Allows you to protect any changes made to specific terrain objects from the synchronization process. Note that this only works if you keep the original names.
    

*   **Reset Materials**
    
    Allows you to protect any changes made to specific material layers from the synchronization process. Note that this only works if you keep the original names!
    

*   **Renderer**
    
    Allows selection of the render engine used by the bridge for material creation.
    
    *   Standard - uses color-based shaders exclusively, without support for layers
        
    *   Redshift - complete support for layers
        
    *   Octane - supports up to 12 layers of materials
        
    

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/export/bridge-tools/cinema-4d-bridge#workflow-example)

**Workflow Example**


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

This example demonstrates how to render terrain in Cinema 4D using Octane. The Canyon sample file that comes with World Creator will be used. These steps can be applied to any other World Creator project.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/export/bridge-tools/cinema-4d-bridge#sync-from-world-creator)

**Sync from World Creator**

Click the sync button in the application bar at the top of the main panel to export all necessary data from World Creator automatically.

![](https://docs.world-creator.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2837684122-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FM6zsxw2jbMYEZbKqEwpa%252Fuploads%252FUvwccwFp3frQSR6fSBf8%252Fwalkthrough_bridge_terrain.webp%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df208acd0-1a26-4e20-9532-4c722bc60871&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d3923a4f&sv=2)

_The World Creator scene before the sync_

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/export/bridge-tools/cinema-4d-bridge#sync-into-cinema-4d)

**Sync into Cinema 4D**

To open the bridge interface in Cinema 4D, select **World Creator Bridge** from the **Extensions** menu. Select Octane as the renderer and click on the **Synchronize** button.

![](https://docs.world-creator.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2837684122-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FM6zsxw2jbMYEZbKqEwpa%252Fuploads%252F5s7VVPjvESeaBxyG74Ut%252Fwalkthrough_bridge_cinema_01.webp%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4f9a8f47-7d18-41a7-8057-1eddf5e0696c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=dea54c6&sv=2)

_Synced terrain in Cinema 4D_

Since we had **Import Layers** activated we now have all material layers from World Creator as individual submaterials, which we can further modify in Cinema 4D.

circle-info

Please note that the Octane bridge can support a maximum of 12 layers.

To add a winter look to the terrain, transform the top sediment layer into snow. Do this by selecting the Sediment material and adding a MixTexture node with a white color RgbSpectrum between the colormap and the output. Although World Creator could provide a more accurate result, we will keep the process within Cinema 4D for the purpose of this guide.

circle-info

Tip: Right-click on a node and choose Auto-arrange to simplify material cleanup.

![](https://docs.world-creator.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2837684122-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FM6zsxw2jbMYEZbKqEwpa%252Fuploads%252FGZzb8UPKchC7dDPX6FLJ%252Fwalkthrough_bridge_cinema_02.webp%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbe2c77dd-ecc1-4d03-bad5-db1640483a4b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=175a3e22&sv=2)

_Synced terrain with altered splat maps in Cinema 4D_

The terrain should now look something like this.

One significant advantage of utilizing the bridge is the faster iteration speed achieved between World Creator and Cinema 4D. To demonstrate this concept more effectively, modify the seed of the entire terrain within World Creator to 1. Doing so will create a different scene that adheres to the same design patterns as our original terrain.

To preserve the snow cover changes in our Cinema 4D materials, we need to deactivate the **Reset Materials** parameter in the bridge options. The bridge subsequently scans the terrain materials for existing subgroups and retains any changes made to them, while also reloading all the relevant new textures. It is crucial to preserve the original names of the subgroups for this to work.

Although we are using this for a relatively simple modification, it is possible to use this feature with more complex materials such as tri-planar shaders while maintaining the same iteration speed between World Creator and Cinema 4D.

circle-info

The same workflow is also available on the object level, where you can add additional modifiers to the terrain mesh or even make changes to the mesh itself. The only condition is that you retain the Subdivision and Displacer modifiers along with the original mesh name.

![](https://docs.world-creator.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2837684122-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FM6zsxw2jbMYEZbKqEwpa%252Fuploads%252FxrJvdQhLzhx4YREg6NXk%252Fwalkthrough_bridge_cinema_03.webp%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0bf781f4-3298-4f24-a7ac-14bd5c19ad40&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e4a4707e&sv=2)

_Material changes applied to a freshly imported terrain with a different seed_

After modifying the seed and resyncing the terrain into Cinema 4D, you should now see the image above.

Last updated 1 year ago

# Debris | World Creator

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/simulation-layers/debris#overview)

Overview


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Debris Simulation adds larger amounts of individual particles to your terrain using a physics simulation. The particles are spawned based on a density value per level step, unlike the other simulation layers. Gravity and interactions with each other affect them, creating a realistic distribution across the terrain.

Spawning debris on all levels allows for a greater variety of element sizes. This means that debris spawned on lower levels will be much larger than debris spawned on higher levels, creating a more natural ratio between large boulders and smaller pebbles.

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/simulation-layers/debris#video-guide)

Video Guide


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

World Creator Guide

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/simulation-layers/debris#parameters)

Parameters


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Properties

Description

**Density**

The spawn density of debris on the terrain.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/simulation-layers/debris#simulation)

Simulation

Properties

Description

**Delta**

The time step delta of the simulation. Can be used to speed it up or slow it down (in relation to the iterations).

**Friction**

The amount of friction that will be applied to the debris.

**Acceleration**

How fast the elements accelerate on the terrain.

**Collision Bounce**

Controls the strength of the reaction when colliding with another particle.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/simulation-layers/debris#shape)

Shape

Properties

Description

**Insert Level**

The level in which the simulated debris will be added to the terrain. Densities on levels above the insert level will be ignored!

**Shape**

Offers you a variety of different shapes, from imported textures and meshes to procedural 2d splats.

**Texture/Model**

Reference to your custom linked texture/model.

**Shape Detail Amp**

Noise scaling for the procedural shapes.

**Height**

Height multiplier for all rendered elements.

**Size**

Range of randomized size of all rendered elements.

**Rotation**

Range of randomized rotation of all rendered elements.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/simulation-layers/debris#tint)

Tint

Properties

Description

**Gradient**

Allows you to apply additional coloring to your distributed debris. To see this on your terrain you have to have a material with "Use Shape Layer Color" enabled. For more info on the gradient itself please refer to the info in the [Gradient Materialarrow-up-right](https://bitethebytes.freshdesk.com/en/support/solutions/articles/44002478305)
.

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/simulation-layers/debris#results)

Results


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.world-creator.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2837684122-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FM6zsxw2jbMYEZbKqEwpa%252Fuploads%252FTqv9sPJPYG0xVI6o1lWg%252Fwalkthrough_simulations_debris_01.webp%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df964e1f6-2666-4cef-94c3-bc6b6cc40ad2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=474519c&sv=2)

![](https://docs.world-creator.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2837684122-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FM6zsxw2jbMYEZbKqEwpa%252Fuploads%252FY8MPowU7THDsvTnvQKU4%252Fwalkthrough_simulations_debris_02.webp%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D38b4b57b-7233-4722-9a77-716a09c7f4c2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e30f0145&sv=2)

# Snow | World Creator

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/simulation-layers/snow#overview)

Overview


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Snow Simulation Layer simulates the evolution of the snow layer over time on the terrain. The system works internally on two separate layers, an upper layer for powdery snow, which is susceptible to diffusion, and a lower unstable layer, which is transformed by avalanches.

Both are affected by melting (powdery snow melts first, as soon as there is no more powdery snow, the unstable snow melts) and, depending on the **Powdery/Unstable Ratio** parameter, also by precipitation.

The key to properly using the snow simulation is to understand the underlying temperature parameters that affect precipitation and melting. Temperature is primarily calculated from elevation. The **Temperature Offset** controls the height at which the temperature is 0°. The **Temperature Scale** then controls how many meters of elevation it takes to change the temperature by one degree (e.g. a scale of 5 means 1° change every 5 meters of elevation). In addition to elevation, the amount of sunlight during the day also affects the temperature. If enabled, the system will use the global sun settings from World Creator, but you can override them if you wish.

The amount of simulated material is also quite different from the other simulation layers, as the snow simulation can produce additional sediment during the simulation, instead of the fixed amount of sediment that is set at a specified spawn level like in the fluid or sand simulation layers.

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/simulation-layers/snow#video-guide)

Video Guide


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

World Creator Guide

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/simulation-layers/snow#parameters)

Parameters


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/simulation-layers/snow#global)

Global

Properties

Description

**Temperature Offset**

The altitude at which the temperature is 0°.

**Temperature Scale**

How many meters of elevation it takes to change 1°.

**Use Global Sun**

Toggles between World Creator's global sun parameter and the layer's custom north value.

**Sun North** (only visible is Use Global Sun is disabled)

The layers custom north value.

**Sun Temperature**

The influence of the terrain's solar exposure on the computed temperature map.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/simulation-layers/snow#precipitation)

Precipitation

Properties

Description

**Strength**

The amount of snowfall in each simulation step.

**Temperature**

The temperature below which precipitation occurs.

**Powdery/Unstable Ratio**

The distribution of powdery/unstable snow in new snowfall. 0 is only powdery, 1 is only unstable snow.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/simulation-layers/snow#melt)

Melt

Properties

Description

**Strength**

The power of the melt in each simulation step.

**Temperature**

The temperature at which melting occurs.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/simulation-layers/snow#diffusion-powdery-layer)

Diffusion (powdery layer)

Properties

Description

**Speed**

The rate of downward diffusion of the powder layer.

**Rest Angle**

Controls the rest angle at which diffusion stops.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/simulation-layers/snow#avalanche-unstable-layer)

Avalanche (unstable layer)

Properties

Description

**Probability**

The probability that an avalanche is formed. Depends on temperature, amount of snow and slope.

**Speed**

The speed at which the avalanches travel downhill.

**Viscosity**

The viscosity/inertia of the avalanche.

**Rest Angle**

The angle at which the avalanche will stop.

**Spawn Level**

In which level the sediment gets added to the terrain.

**Spawn Amount**

The amount of sediment added to the terrain.

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/simulation-layers/snow#result)

Result


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.world-creator.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2837684122-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FM6zsxw2jbMYEZbKqEwpa%252Fuploads%252F9fTkv8urvU2VAYbDCFjR%252Fwalkthrough_simulations_snow_01.webp%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9f4692f2-8a27-4997-bfe3-31a0af572c2c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6799cbde&sv=2)

![](https://docs.world-creator.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2837684122-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FM6zsxw2jbMYEZbKqEwpa%252Fuploads%252Fz38hnFwBR0fVVRK6R4b7%252Fwalkthrough_simulations_snow_02.webp%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D99dd45bb-1314-41a2-8c87-2b4920125627&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d795fe27&sv=2)

# Simulation Layers | World Creator

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/simulation-layers#overview)

Overview


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Simulation layers provide a brand-new method to alter your terrain by utilizing extensive matter-based physics simulations for your World Creator terrains.

Each simulation layer is linked with a sediment layer, which stores the produced matter and upsamples it similarly to World Creator's base terrain with the [level steps system](https://docs.world-creator.com/walkthrough/terrain-setup/level-step-system)
. Then, each stage can continue to further simulate the sediment, providing the highest fidelity result at every resolution while also interacting with the filter system.

It's important to note that the area you set in the properties only refers to the spawning area. The simulation can go beyond the boundaries, allowing you to position sediment emitters on the terrain and let World Creator take care of the sediment's or fluid's realistic placement.

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/simulation-layers#shared-parameters)

Shared Parameters


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

All simulation layers have the following several features in common:

![](https://docs.world-creator.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2837684122-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FM6zsxw2jbMYEZbKqEwpa%252Fuploads%252FnJyF0ClCaMY8If9qDgN8%252Freference_simulations_information_02.webp%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc02b4028-4451-47c4-82a2-9862b148f8ca&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6bfafe41&sv=2)

*   **Show Mask** Shows the mask on the terrain.
    
*   **Import/Export** Allows you to import or export the mask.
    
*   **Edit** Allows you to edit the mask using brushes.
    
*   **Spawn Level** The level in which the sediment will be inserted on the terrain.
    
*   **Spawn Amount** The amount of sediment that will be spawned.
    
*   **Iterations** How many iterations the simulation will run for. Offers control for each level step.
    

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/simulation-layers#available-simulation-layers)

Available Simulation Layers


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

World Creator currently offers the following simulations:

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/simulation-layers#sand-simulation)

Sand Simulation

This [Sand Simulation](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/simulation-layers/sand)
 simulates granular materials. It simulates the given matter with a particle-based system that moves the material from an unstable position downhill until a stable state is achieved and in the process fills up crevices and cracks.

![](https://docs.world-creator.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2837684122-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FM6zsxw2jbMYEZbKqEwpa%252Fuploads%252Fta1qFO8hYua7OrGdFg5V%252Fwalkthrough_simulations_sand_01.webp%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7bece237-3330-4284-a794-85dc9c11bb8c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d1058320&sv=2)

sedimentation

![](https://docs.world-creator.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2837684122-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FM6zsxw2jbMYEZbKqEwpa%252Fuploads%252FLDgEC7palpgRhQD7NO5Z%252Fwalkthrough_simulations_sand_02.webp%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5f18afa3-1119-4b0c-ab6a-c3bb5bf40ef9&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f2d85713&sv=2)

painting sedimentation onto the terrain

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/simulation-layers#fluid-simulation)

Fluid Simulation

The [Fluid Simulation](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/simulation-layers/fluid)
 allows you to run a fluid simulation on your terrain in World Creator. Depending on the parameters it can be used to simulate basic water movement or other thicker liquids like lava. Additionally, it can be used to fill local depressions and thereby create lakes on your terrain which can then be textured with the **Simulation Layer distribution**.

![](https://docs.world-creator.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2837684122-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FM6zsxw2jbMYEZbKqEwpa%252Fuploads%252FmO5JE9VZgaAwYEZfVVgm%252Fwalkthrough_simulations_fluid_02.webp%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df12451e3-c7ad-4fc0-8dea-8f5b09a771f0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ab93527a&sv=2)

fluid running down a mountain

![](https://docs.world-creator.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2837684122-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FM6zsxw2jbMYEZbKqEwpa%252Fuploads%252FWO7lcS32RptC7r9wyUKf%252Fwalkthrough_simulations_fluid_01.webp%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3e2f2d1e-5be1-4224-adc8-dae24b08f951&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1d499c4&sv=2)

the simulation creates lakes in natural depressions

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/simulation-layers#snow-simulation)

Snow Simulation

The [Snow Simulation](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/simulation-layers/snow)
 adds a thermal snow simulation to your terrain, that simulates snow downfall, melting, diffusion and avalanches.

![](https://docs.world-creator.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2837684122-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FM6zsxw2jbMYEZbKqEwpa%252Fuploads%252F9fTkv8urvU2VAYbDCFjR%252Fwalkthrough_simulations_snow_01.webp%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9f4692f2-8a27-4997-bfe3-31a0af572c2c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6799cbde&sv=2)

![](https://docs.world-creator.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2837684122-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FM6zsxw2jbMYEZbKqEwpa%252Fuploads%252Fz38hnFwBR0fVVRK6R4b7%252Fwalkthrough_simulations_snow_02.webp%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D99dd45bb-1314-41a2-8c87-2b4920125627&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d795fe27&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/simulation-layers#debris-simulation)

Debris Simulation

The [Debris Simulation](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/simulation-layers/debris)
 simulates larger particles on your terrain. Unlike most other simulation layers, it doesn't work with a set **spawn amount** that is inserted and then simulated, but instead adds a set number of elements at each level step (which also controls their size). Particles can be anything from procedural 2D splats to custom imported textures or even full 3D meshes.

![](https://docs.world-creator.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2837684122-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FM6zsxw2jbMYEZbKqEwpa%252Fuploads%252FTqv9sPJPYG0xVI6o1lWg%252Fwalkthrough_simulations_debris_01.webp%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df964e1f6-2666-4cef-94c3-bc6b6cc40ad2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=474519c&sv=2)

![](https://docs.world-creator.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2837684122-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FM6zsxw2jbMYEZbKqEwpa%252Fuploads%252FY8MPowU7THDsvTnvQKU4%252Fwalkthrough_simulations_debris_02.webp%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D38b4b57b-7233-4722-9a77-716a09c7f4c2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e30f0145&sv=2)

[PreviousHole Layerschevron-left](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/hole-layers)
[NextFluidchevron-right](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/simulation-layers/fluid)

# Objects | World Creator

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/biome/objects#overview)

Overview


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Object Layer allows you to add procedural objects to your biomes. It offers vast customizability for object placement, scaling and density as well as material enhancement to perfectly match your scene.

![](https://docs.world-creator.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2837684122-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FM6zsxw2jbMYEZbKqEwpa%252Fuploads%252FM03jIwPOidfLxuJOEfCT%252Freference_objects_01.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc9f534a1-7677-4edf-be2a-b7475b43421a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9d5a045a&sv=2)

![](https://docs.world-creator.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2837684122-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FM6zsxw2jbMYEZbKqEwpa%252Fuploads%252FaEo9HbRY57PkbDTsoaXl%252Fwalkthrough_terrains_17.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6497073c-8145-4d53-bc9e-e135ec6285f4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bb68de84&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/biome/objects#sub-objects)

Sub Objects


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Sub Objects allow you to place objects in the vicinity of a main object. This can be useful to get certain proximity setups like mushrooms around a tree stump or other features.

![](https://docs.world-creator.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2837684122-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FM6zsxw2jbMYEZbKqEwpa%252Fuploads%252Flh3uvujuuSsl0tu4XA3A%252Freference_objects_sub.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dff5c3270-b4ca-4e33-b20a-c5447d0898d6&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ac7d82a0&sv=2)

Plants and mushrooms placed as sub objects around a tree stump

Properties

Description

**Radius**

Controls the lower/upper limit for the radius around an object where subobjects can be spawned.

**Amount**

The number of instances spawned as subobjects.

**Denisty**

Density multiplier for the subobjects.

**Seed**

The seed for the placement of subobjects.

**Percentage**

The percentage of the all sub objects of the main object that this sub object takes up.

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/biome/objects#distribution-settings)

Distribution Settings


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Property

Description

**Seed**

The seed used for procedural distribution.

**Instance Distance**

The distance between instances.

**Overwrite Radius**

**Overwrite Radius Smooth**

**Density**

Modifies the density of the scattered objects.

**Push**

Pushes the meshes from their base positions to create a more scattered result.

**Height Offset**

Offsets the objects along the up axis of the terrain.

**Normal Offset**

Offsets the objects along the normal at the current position.

**Uniform Scaling**

Switches between uniform and individual axis scaling.

**Scale Range/X/Y/Z**

Controls the upper/lower limit of the scale of the object.

**Align to Normal**

Align the up axis of the object to the normal of the terrain.

**Rotation Range X/Y/Z**

Controls the upper/lower limit of the rotation of the object.

**Use Distribution Density**

Links the density to the distribution of the object layer. This allows you to fade out the density if wanted.

**Use Distribution Scale**

Links the scale of the objects to the distribution of the object layer. This allows you to fade out the scale if wanted.

**Use Distribution Gradient**

Links the material gradient to the distribution of the object layer. This allows you to color your objects procedurally based on your distribution.

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/biome/objects#object-settings)

Object Settings


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Property

Description

**Object Type**

This setting is crucial for exporting. 'Instance' will export and synchronise your object as a point cloud, while 'Detail' will export your object as a mask that can be used procedurally for scattering in your renderer.

**Is Entity**

Allows you to mark instances as entities. This setting is important for certain bridge exports where these objects will then be spawned as e.g. GameObjects in Unity.

**Model**

The object that should be distributed on your terrain. The recommended format is .glb but .gltf, .fbx and .obj are also supported.

**Model Scale**

Controls the scale of the model.

**Model Y Axis**

Sets the y axis of the model. This helps when bringing in an object that has a different up axis.

**Materials**

Shows you all materials the imported object has and lets you individually modify them.

**Tint**

Tints the color of the material.

**Use Gradient**

Enables the gradient for this object. The full gradient parameter explanation can be found in the [materials article](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/biome/materials)
.

**Normal Strength**

Controls the strength of the normal map.

**Flip Normal Y**

Inverts the up channel of the normal map.

**Roughness**

Controls the roughness of the material.

**Roughness Map Factor**

Controls the influence of the roughness map.

**Metalness**

Controls the metalness of the material.

**Metalness Map Factor**

Controls the influence of the metalness map.

**Uses Gloss Map**

Switches to a gloss material shader.

**Emission Strength**

Controls the emissive strength of the material.

**Two Sided**

Renders the backfaces for the given material. This is crucial for the leaves of foliage as otherwise the backfaces will be culled.

**Alpha Mode**

Allows you to switch between several alpha modes.

**Terrain Blending**

Blends the material of the terrain onto the object based on height.

[PreviousMaterialschevron-left](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/biome/materials)
[NextBiome Layerschevron-right](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/biome-layers)

Last updated 5 months ago

Was this helpful?

*   [Overview](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/biome/objects#overview)
    
*   [Sub Objects](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/biome/objects#sub-objects)
    
*   [Distribution Settings](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/biome/objects#distribution-settings)
    
*   [Object Settings](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/biome/objects#object-settings)
    

Was this helpful?

# 빠른 흐름 | World Creator

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/ko/reference/terrain/effects/fast-flow#undefined)

개요


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Fast Flow 효과는 유체 입자 시뮬레이션을 실행하고 그로부터 마스크를 생성합니다.

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/ko/reference/terrain/effects/fast-flow#undefined-1)

매개변수


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

속성

설명

**반복 횟수**

시뮬레이션이 실행될 반복 횟수입니다.

**속도 임계값**

이 값보다 속도가 낮은 입자는 제거됩니다.

**비 강도**

시뮬레이션 시작 시 떨어뜨리는 비 입자의 수입니다.

**부드러움**

결과 마스크를 부드럽게 합니다.

**흐름 컷오프**

일정량 이하의 물을 가진 모든 입자를 제거합니다.

**흐름 부드러움**

개별 흐름 사이의 부드러운 영역을 혼합합니다.

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/ko/reference/terrain/effects/fast-flow#undefined-2)

결과


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.world-creator.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1093768915-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FM6zsxw2jbMYEZbKqEwpa%252Fuploads%252FZQ3XhFhDO2Xuc1lLwGOi%252Freference_effects_base.webp%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D231bbbf1-25f7-4ffd-b3ee-8772efa06d27&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a4f88c3e&sv=2)

![](https://docs.world-creator.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1093768915-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FM6zsxw2jbMYEZbKqEwpa%252Fuploads%252F4xQeYHV0EPDQkXS5urk5%252Freference_effects_fastflow_02.webp%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De9c27e48-41a2-429d-8d18-fe1d4c9dead2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4e8222b1&sv=2)

마지막 업데이트 5개월 전

도움이 되었나요?

# 효과 | World Creator

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/ko/reference/terrain/effects#undefined)

개요


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

World Creator의 이펙트는 모든 분포에 추가할 수 있어 분포 결과를 더 수정할 수 있습니다.

이펙트로 얻을 수 있는 결과는 다양하며, 다음과 같습니다. [각도 블러](https://docs.world-creator.com/ko/reference/terrain/effects/blur)
, [클램프](https://docs.world-creator.com/ko/reference/terrain/effects/clamp)
 [](https://docs.world-creator.com/ko/reference/terrain/distributions/terrain/curvature)
또는 [노이즈 제거](https://docs.world-creator.com/ko/reference/terrain/effects/denoise)
 마스크에서부터 더 복잡한 것들까지 [심플 플로우](https://docs.world-creator.com/ko/reference/terrain/effects/simple-flow)
.

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/ko/reference/terrain/effects#undefined-1)

**이펙트 사용하기**


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

이펙트를 추가하려면 이펙트 레이블 옆의 작은 더하기 아이콘을 누르세요.

![](https://docs.world-creator.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1093768915-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FM6zsxw2jbMYEZbKqEwpa%252Fuploads%252Fe4JtumR6yb1G4KS8f3rO%252Fwalkthrough_effects_01.webp%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbba2d24c-6bdc-4a54-91a2-78cd967efb96&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7578bdb0&sv=2)

World Creator의 [필터 시스템](https://docs.world-creator.com/ko/reference/terrain/biome/filters)
과 유사하게, 이펙트는 레이어 스택에서 작동하며 아래에서 위로 적용됩니다.

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/ko/reference/terrain/effects#undefined-2)

**공통 파라미터**


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

모든 이펙트는 다음 옵션을 제공합니다:

*   **불투명도** 이펙트의 강도입니다.
    

*   **가중치** 다른 이펙트에 대한 영향을 줄일 수 있습니다.
    

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/ko/reference/terrain/effects#undefined-3)

사용 가능한 이펙트


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

# 3D Stamp | World Creator

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/shape-layers/3d-stamp#overview)

Overview


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The 3D Stamp layer allows you to import your own custom 3D models into World Creator and integrate them into your final terrain creation. In addition to simply adding it to the height map, World Creator also allows you to seamlessly blend its materials into your color maps.

![](https://docs.world-creator.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2837684122-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FM6zsxw2jbMYEZbKqEwpa%252Fuploads%252FuLQiraLtlFOtWV8QOKln%252Freference_shapelayers_3dstamp_01.webp%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D116defde-0fd5-4ea3-8bb6-62e81620e4cb&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e44713b6&sv=2)

3D stamp layer

![](https://docs.world-creator.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2837684122-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FM6zsxw2jbMYEZbKqEwpa%252Fuploads%252F8ivf9XqREoPsfsztIDmH%252Freference_shapelayers_3dstamp_02.webp%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc9da0498-c6ee-4152-8be5-653651acbebe&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3d69407c&sv=2)

3D stamp layer with multiple instances

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/shape-layers/3d-stamp#video-guide)

Video Guide


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

World Creator Guide

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/shape-layers/3d-stamp#hotkeys)

Hotkeys


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The following hotkeys are available in **EDIT** mode:

Add Model Instance

SHIFT + Left Mouse

Remove Model Instance

CTRL + Right Mouse

Select Model Instance

Left Mouse

Translation Mode

T

Rotation Mode

R

Scaling Mode

Z or Y

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/shape-layers/3d-stamp#parameters)

Parameters


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **Model** Allows you to reference the model you want to load.

# Dots | World Creator

* * *

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/distributions/pattern/dots#overview)

Overview


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Dots distribution creates a selection of a grid of dots on your terrain.

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/distributions/pattern/dots#parameters)

Parameters


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   **Smoothness** Smoothly blends the dots onto the terrain.
    

*   **Amount** Controls the scale of the dot grid.
    

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/distributions/pattern/dots#results)
