# Blender Bridge | World Creator

The World Creator Bridge for Blender allows you to seamlessly import your terrain creations into Blender for use in your Blender projects.

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/export/bridge-tools/blender-bridge#installation)

**Installation**


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Drag and drop the .zip file laying in the same directory as the ReadMe into Blender and press “OK” on the installation panel.

To open the bridge interface in Blender open the Sidebar in the 3D Viewport or press “N” while hovering over the 3D Viewport and select “WCBridge”.

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/export/bridge-tools/blender-bridge#parameters)

Parameters


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/export/bridge-tools/blender-bridge#terrain)

**Terrain**

In this tab you can import your terrain. All other steps in the bridge require a terrain to be imported first since they all build up on it.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/export/bridge-tools/blender-bridge#import)

Import

Properties

Description

**XML File**

Locate the .xml file for the desired sync project. For WC 22 and above, this file is located by default at _\[User\]_\\Documents\\World Creator\\Sync\\

**Prefix**

Specify the prefix for all terrain objects and collections created by the bridge. Modify this parameter if you intend to import a second terrain, otherwise, the old one will be overwritten.

**Import Layers**

Switch between using individual terrain layers or a baked colormap in the generated material.

**Adjust Clipping**

Automatically adjusts the clipping distance of the viewport camera to ensure the whole terrain is visible. (Specifically changes the viewpoint camera and not the rendering camera!)

**Reset Terrain**

Allows you to protect any changes made to specific terrain objects from the synchronization process. Note that this only works if you keep the original names!

**Reset Materials**

Allows you to protect any changes made to specific material layers from the synchronization process. Note that this only works if you keep the original names!

**Output**

Allows you to switch between Blenders Cycles/Eevee or the output used for modding packages. Currently "Modding" only support GTA V specific Sollumz.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/export/bridge-tools/blender-bridge#parameters-1)

**Parameters**

Properties

Description

**World Scale**

This parameter determines the scale factor for the terrain. (Default: 1 pixel in World Coordinates in width equals 1 meter in Blender)

**Height Scale**

Specifies the factor for scaling the height of the terrain.

**Interpolation**

Enables height-map interpolation. Interpolation is only applied on single-tile terrains by default, as it results in artifacts on the seams of multi-tile terrains.

**Auto Subdivision**

The subdivision of the generated mesh is automatically adjusted to the resolution of the synchronized heightmap to reduce sampling artifacts.

**Subd Viewport/Render**

The level of terrain subdivision can be set.

**Vertex Reduction**

Adds a Decimate Modifier to the mesh. 0 means no decimation, 1 full reduction.

**Merge Tiles**

Combines all individual terrain tiles into one mesh to get rid of any seams.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/export/bridge-tools/blender-bridge#objects)

**Objects**

With the arrival of WC 2025.1 you can now also sync your scattered objects into Blender using the WC Bridge. The bridge uses Geometry Nodes to distribute point cloud based and procedurally masked objects on your terrain. All parameters can be found below.

circle-info

If you don't see any objects after syncing this could be because Frustum Culling and Distance Culling for all systems above the instance threshold is enabled by default to prevent performance crashes after syncing a large scene.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/export/bridge-tools/blender-bridge#import-1)

Import

Properties

Description

**Reset Objects**

Overwrite all modifications made to objects on Import. This resets all objects back to the exported ones from WC.

**Frustum Instance Threshold**

Systems with an instance count above this threshold will have frustum culling enabled by default.

**Base Frustum Margin**

The default Frustum Mmargin used on every created system.

**Base Distance Start/End**

The default Distance Culling Start/End point used on every created system.

**Sync**

Loads the objects from your synced WC project.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/export/bridge-tools/blender-bridge#systems)

Systems

Shows you all available systems of the current terrain. You can add new ones with objects from your blender project, remove systems, sort/rename them and change their visibility in the viewport/render as well as quickly toggle the proxy status.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/export/bridge-tools/blender-bridge#system)

System

Properties

Description

**Object Identifier**

A randomized identifier used for this object to differentiate objects from WC that have the same name. Automatically set up on sync.

**Object Collection**

The collection where the object that should be scattered is stored. There can be multiple objects in a collection, allowing you to use randomized variations in case you need it :)

**Model Scale**

The converted Modelscale from World Creator. Is automatically set on sync.

**Distribution Type**

Allows you to switch between Point Cloud and Procedural scattering. This is based on the **Distribution Type** in WC.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/export/bridge-tools/blender-bridge#display)

Display

Properties

Description

**Only Frustum**

If enabled the density reduction is only applied to systems that use frustum culling.

**Density Reduction**

Applies a multiplier (0-1) to the density/pointclouds of all systems.

**Use Active Camera**

Allows you to specify the camera that is used for distance/frustum culling.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/export/bridge-tools/blender-bridge#export)

Export

Properties

Description

**Include Culled Instances**

Includes currently culled objects in the export.

**Realize selected System**

Exports all instances of the currently selected system.

**Realize all Systems**

Exports the instances of all systems of the terrain.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/export/bridge-tools/blender-bridge#modding)

Modding

The blender bridge supports terrain conversion for GTAV. This comes in the form of getting the terrain set up to be exported using Sollumz into Codewalker where you can then use it on your own GTAV server. Support for other modding platforms will be added in the future :)

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/export/bridge-tools/blender-bridge#sollumz)

Sollumz

The Sollumz terrain material setup is quite specific, requiring a mesh where materials are blended using the green and blue channels of the second vertex colours, with a maximum of four different textures blended on each polygon. This would work well for a few materials, but you'll probably have more than four. The solution is to find the strongest material on each face, create a unique material combination for it, and then assign the vertex colours based on our splat map data and combination order. The bridge does exactly that, but there's a catch: you can only use up to three individual materials for each blend, because of how vertex colour blending works. You could achieve the full four-material blend by hand painting and assigning it, but that could take up to several months of work for a developer. While slightly more materials should just be a minor performance compromise, it's still something to consider.

To get a nice result we advise to use the unpacked .dds textures from Codewalker directly in World Creator (WC materials support the .dds file type).

circle-info

A demo video on this feature will come soon! :)

Properties

Description

**Collision Mesh**

Creates a collision mesh with where only the strongest material on a face is assigned. This can then easily be replaced using **Sollumz** \-> **Create Collision Material** \-> **Convert to Selected** to assign the correct collision materials.

**Create Drawable**

This packs the collision mesh and terrain mesh into a ready to export drawable. (You still have to assign collision materials as described above)

**Convert Terrain**

Converts the terrain to be ready for Codewalker.

**UV0 Scale**

Adjusts the uv scale of the texture maps. The whole terrain only has one texture uv scale.

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/export/bridge-tools/blender-bridge#workflow-example)

**Workflow Example**


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Video

Written

This example illustrates the process of syncing a terrain into Blender using v1 of the bridge. The Canyon sample file that comes with World Creator will be used for this purpose. These steps can be applied to any other World Creator project.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/export/bridge-tools/blender-bridge#sync-from-world-creator)

**Sync from World Creator**

Click the sync button in the application bar at the top of the main panel to export all necessary data from World Creator automatically.

![](https://docs.world-creator.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2837684122-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FM6zsxw2jbMYEZbKqEwpa%252Fuploads%252FUvwccwFp3frQSR6fSBf8%252Fwalkthrough_bridge_terrain.webp%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df208acd0-1a26-4e20-9532-4c722bc60871&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d3923a4f&sv=2)

_The World Creator scene before the sync_

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/export/bridge-tools/blender-bridge#sync-into-blender)

**Sync into Blender**

To open the bridge interface, press **N** in the viewing area and select 'WC Bridge' from the sidebar on the right. Then, click on the **Synchronize** button located at the bottom of the panel.

![](https://docs.world-creator.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2837684122-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FM6zsxw2jbMYEZbKqEwpa%252Fuploads%252FRqQhZ0VvkgPzAbzeT6mr%252Fwalkthrough_bridge_blender_01.webp%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0bfe5ac8-6faf-4775-9202-c81d9a42fe5e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=de5f485b&sv=2)

_Synced terrain in Blender_

Since the **Import Layers** option was activated, all material layers from World Creator are now available as separate groups that can be modified further within Blender.

To give our terrain a winter look, we will transform the top sediment layer to resemble snow. To do this, open the **Sediment** subgroup and add a **Mix** node with a white color between the color map and the output. Although we could achieve a more precise outcome using World Creator, we will stick to Blender for the purpose of this guide.

![](https://docs.world-creator.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2837684122-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FM6zsxw2jbMYEZbKqEwpa%252Fuploads%252FSm7TPsI1o5xlV2iW1W7H%252Fwalkthrough_bridge_blender_02.webp%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D73876aff-3e02-4b41-bdab-cdfbfdba1d37&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8a8c33f5&sv=2)

_Synced terrain with altered splat maps in Blender_

The terrain should now appear as shown in the picture.

A significant advantage of using the bridge is the enhanced iteration speed between World Creator and Blender that it offers. To demonstrate this more clearly, alter the terrain's seed value to 1 in World Creator, resulting in a new scene that adheres to the original terrain's design patterns.

To preserve the snow cover modifications in our Blender material, we must deactivate the Reset Materials parameters in the bridge settings. The bridge consequently scans the terrain materials for existing subgroups, retaining any changes made to them in tandem with reloading all appropriate new textures. To make this work, you must retain the original names of the subgroups.

circle-info

You can use the same workflow at the object level, where you are able to include more modifiers to the terrain mesh. For this purpose, you must keep the Subdivision and Displace modifiers and the original mesh name.

![](https://docs.world-creator.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2837684122-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FM6zsxw2jbMYEZbKqEwpa%252Fuploads%252Fuq6RY1Mdve5L2Ovx7494%252Fwalkthrough_bridge_blender_03.webp%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd89722a8-b37a-420b-a02f-f97bbc26d676&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=29c3f869&sv=2)

_Material changes applied to a freshly imported terrain with a different seed_

Last updated 1 month ago

# 2D Stamp | World Creator

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/shape-layers/2d-stamp#overview)

Overview


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

With stamp layers, you can import custom height maps into World Creator and blend them seamlessly into your terrains. The following images showcase the effects of various level steps and the decreasing impact of erosion has on the higher levels.

![](https://docs.world-creator.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2837684122-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FM6zsxw2jbMYEZbKqEwpa%252Fuploads%252FZ8pHYB8rkUObzLP4uGPK%252Freference_shapelayers_2dstamp_01.webp%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df921aa63-11c7-4f00-a83a-b3b286d79692&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a57ff3e1&sv=2)

low level

![](https://docs.world-creator.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2837684122-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FM6zsxw2jbMYEZbKqEwpa%252Fuploads%252FZCgXd2wNsQeWoXB8E86Q%252Freference_shapelayers_2dstamp_02.webp%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D254bece4-3acc-4e61-92a5-d7e99a9932b9&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=af953117&sv=2)

medium level

![](https://docs.world-creator.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2837684122-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FM6zsxw2jbMYEZbKqEwpa%252Fuploads%252FTJ66nYCZ5QF6QgT0cXp1%252Freference_shapelayers_2dstamp_03.webp%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df12a034c-da23-4d13-9dac-f2b55b665e8f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c4690d1d&sv=2)

high level

circle-info

If your stamp does not appear on the selected [level step](https://docs.world-creator.com/walkthrough/terrain-setup/level-step-system)
, it might be because the level step of your biomes is higher and is therefore overwriting your stamp.

In addition to the level step, you also have area settings that enable you to accurately place and blend your stamp with the existing terrain to enhance your final composition.

![](https://docs.world-creator.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2837684122-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FM6zsxw2jbMYEZbKqEwpa%252Fuploads%252Fw1XfkNlgKax7CAYpWtup%252Freference_shapelayers_2dstamp_04.webp%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2df556cc-0c3c-4d9e-ad63-22c8da6937c7&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3d804b87&sv=2)

2d stamp placed on the terrain

The last important feature of the stamp map is the ability to import color maps in addition to your height map. By default, the color map of a stamp is applied to every material. You can disable it by turning off the option **Use Shape Layer Color** in the material settings. Bear in mind that this setting will also affect all other shape layers, including [MapTiler layers](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/shape-layers/maptiler)
.

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/shape-layers/2d-stamp#video-guides)

Video Guides


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

World Creator Guide

Guide by Design with TP

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/shape-layers/2d-stamp#parameters)

Parameters


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Properties

Description

**Height Map**

Allows you to load in a custom height map.

**Set Height Range**

Allows the usage of a custom height range.

**Color Map**

Can reference an accompanying color map for texturing.

**Saturation**

Adjusts the saturation of the color map.

**Contrast**

Adjusts the contrast of the color map.

**Brightness**

Adjusts the brightness of the color map.

**Flip X/Y**

Flips the stamp in the X or Y direction.

**Create Sculpt Layer**

Converts the 2d Stamp layer into a sculpt layer for further design work

# Path | World Creator

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/shape-layers/path#overview)

Overview


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Path layers modify terrain based on custom paths set up in World Creator. This feature enables the building of various structures like mountains, valleys, rivers, or streets.

![](https://docs.world-creator.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2837684122-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FM6zsxw2jbMYEZbKqEwpa%252Fuploads%252FCP5etyZMx9TF4pHqFVZr%252Freference_shapelayers_path_01.webp%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbbb940e7-487b-4322-8b35-cfa414b17c1d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6a73b175&sv=2)

building a road

![](https://docs.world-creator.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2837684122-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FM6zsxw2jbMYEZbKqEwpa%252Fuploads%252FfIMaMD24KrO2XBCApyXj%252Freference_shapelayers_path_02.webp%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc8e7ec29-040b-4ab7-82a2-21de014d1452&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=db6ddc14&sv=2)

final terrain

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/shape-layers/path#video-guide)

Video Guide


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

World Creator Guide

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/shape-layers/path#hotkeys)

Hotkeys


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Affect all nodes at once

(SHIFT)

Add Node

SHIFT + Left Mouse

Move/Scale Node

(SHIFT) + Left Mouse + Drag

Remove Node

(SHIFT) + CTRL + Drag

Change Height

(SHIFT) + ALT + Left Mouse + Drag

Rotate Path

R + Left Mouse + Drag

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/shape-layers/path#parameters)

Parameters


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/shape-layers/path#path-settings)

Path Settings

*   **Width** The base width is multiplied by the width of each control point. If the overall width is 0, individual point widths cannot exceed 0.
    

*   **Falloff** Falloff of the path. This is added to the path width.
    

*   **Falloff Curve** Falloff steepness.
    

*   **Noise Strength** The noise is added to the path width.
    

*   **Noise Scale** Adjusts the noise scale along the path's length.
    

*   **Closed** Connects the first and last control point if enabled.
    

*   **Height Offset** Shifts the whole path upwards or downwards.
    

*   **Flatten** Flattens the heights of all control points.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/shape-layers/path#procedural-width)

Procedural Width

The Procedural Width parameters allows you to automatically set the node widths between the set width range.

*   **Range** The range between which the node widths will be set.
    

*   **Mode** Allows you to select from a bunch of different types like ascending, descending, zigzag or random distribution.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/shape-layers/path#spline-export)

Spline Export

*   Export Spline Allows you to export the spline for usage in a render engine.
    

Last updated 1 year ago

Was this helpful?

*   [Video Guide](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/shape-layers/path#video-guide)
    
*   [Hotkeys](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/shape-layers/path#hotkeys)
    
*   [Parameters](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/shape-layers/path#parameters)
    
*   [Path Settings](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/shape-layers/path#path-settings)

Overview


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Grids distribution creates a grid selection with various parameters.

Parameters


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Properties

Description

**Grid Type**

Changes between horizontal, vertical and combined types.

**Distance**

Scales the whole grid.

**Smoothness**

Smooths the grid lines.

**Thickness**

Controls the thickness of the grid lines.

**Offset X/Z**

Shifts the grid in the x/z direction.

**Rotation**

Rotates the grid.

# Polygon | World Creator

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/shape-layers/polygon#overview)

Overview


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Polygon shape layer allows you to create your own custom polygon and assign a height to its inner and outer edges, allowing you to create flat areas, craters or mountains.

![](https://docs.world-creator.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2837684122-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FM6zsxw2jbMYEZbKqEwpa%252Fuploads%252FQjH1znJp6CQ9zjoOnJyv%252Freference_shapelayers_polygon_01.webp%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D206d980d-1ca0-44b5-b3a6-7713d7a2035f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5b525ae8&sv=2)

flattened area

![](https://docs.world-creator.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2837684122-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FM6zsxw2jbMYEZbKqEwpa%252Fuploads%252FHIo5xdvBd6AY52CNp4g6%252Freference_shapelayers_polygon_02.webp%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D148d6ba1-4eca-4477-941c-de49a06a2c1f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=63876c49&sv=2)

mountain using the polygon layer

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/shape-layers/polygon#video-guide)

Video Guide


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

World Creator Guide

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/shape-layers/polygon#hotkeys)

Hotkeys


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Affect whole shape at once

(SHIFT)

Add Node

SHIFT + Left Mouse

Move Node

(SHIFT) + Left Mouse on Node + Drag

Remove Node

(SHIFT) + CTRL + Right Mouse on Node

Rotate Shape

R + Left Mouse + Drag

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/shape-layers/polygon#parameters)

Parameters


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/shape-layers/polygon#polygon-settings)

Polygon Settings

*   **Seed** The Seed used in the layer.
    

*   **Spline Smoothness** Controls the number of steps for each spline, with a higher count producing a smoother and more rounded shape.
    

*   **Surface Smoothness** Rounds the curvature of the shape.
    

*   **Corner Offset** Rounds and shifts the shape outwards.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/shape-layers/polygon#outside-settings)

Outside Settings

*   **Height Offset** Shifts the height of the polygon.
    

*   **Outer Falloff** Controls the outward falloff of the polygon.
    

*   **Falloff Curve** Adjusts the steepness of the outer falloff.
    

*   **Noise Strength** Adds noise into the outer falloff.
    

*   **Noise Scale** The scale of the added noise.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/shape-layers/polygon#inside-settings)

Inside Settings

*   **Height Offset** Shifts the height of the inner influence area of the polygon.
    

*   **Inside Falloff** Controls the inward falloff of the polygon.
    

*   **Falloff Curve** Adjusts the steepness of the inner falloff.
    

*   **Noise Strength** Adds noise into the inner falloff.
    

*   **Noise Scale** The scale of the added noise.
    

Last updated 1 year ago

*   [Hotkeys](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/shape-layers/polygon#hotkeys)
    
*   [Parameters](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/shape-layers/polygon#parameters)
    
*   [Polygon Settings](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/shape-layers/polygon#polygon-settings)

# Splatter | World Creator

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/distributions/pattern/splatter#overview)

Overview


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Splatter distribution allows you to scatter images onto the terrain to create a selection.

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/distributions/pattern/splatter#parameters)

Parameters


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Properties

Description

**Seed**

The seed is used for randomizing various aspects of the splats.

**Grid Size**

Changes the scale of the underlying grid that is used for scattering.

**Layers**

Allows you to add multiple grid layers, essentially increasing the density of the splats.

**Layer Scale Range**

When having multiple layers their randomized scales can be set with this parameter.

**Size Range**

Randomly multiplies the scale of the individual splats on each layer with a value in this range.

**Position Offset**

Allows you to add a randomized offset to your splats.

**Use Terrain Direction**

If enabled, it aligns your splats to the terrain normals.

**Value Range**

Assign a random value inside the range to each splat.

**Splat Probability**

Allows you to assign each splat a probability of not spawning.

**Texture**

Allows you to reference your own custom splat to be used in the distribution.

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/distributions/pattern/splatter#results)

Results


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.world-creator.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2837684122-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FM6zsxw2jbMYEZbKqEwpa%252Fuploads%252FYbX1Fi0Y9goQSwqMY7Xp%252Freference_distributions_splatter_01.webp%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D539fc921-13e3-442b-8a2f-1c1bcc685f91&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=580f5421&sv=2)

# Maze | World Creator

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/distributions/pattern/maze#overview)

Overview


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The Maze distribution creates a maze pattern.

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/distributions/pattern/maze#parameters)

Parameters


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Properties

Description

**Seed**

Randomizes the pattern seed.

**Distance**

Scales the whole maze pattern.

**Smoothness**

The smoothness of the maze walls.

**Thickness**

The thickness of the maze walls.

**Offset X/Z**

Shifts the maze in the x/z position.

**Rotation**

Rotates the maze pattern.

**Directional Bias**

Shifts between horizontal and vertical wall generation.

**Density**

Removes random wall pieces.

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/distributions/pattern/maze#results)

Results


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

# 작은 흐름 | World Creator

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/ko/reference/terrain/effects/small-flow#undefined)

개요


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

스몰 플로우 효과는 분포를 플로우 방향을 따라 변위시킵니다. 공동 분포(cavity distribution)의 결과처럼 값과 가장자리가 다양하게 분포된 패턴에 가장 잘 작동합니다.

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/ko/reference/terrain/effects/small-flow#undefined-1)

매개변수


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

속성

설명

**강도(Strength)**

플로우 효과의 강도입니다.

**방향**

플로우 효과의 방향입니다.

# MapTiler | World Creator

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/shape-layers/maptiler#overview)

Overview


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The MapTiler Layer enables loading real-world satellite height and color data into World Creator either as a base for your terrain or to improve your procedural creation.

If you're starting out and want to set up MapTiler head over to [this section](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/shape-layers/maptiler#setting-up-maptiler)
.

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/shape-layers/maptiler#video-guide)

Video Guide


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

World Creator Guide

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/shape-layers/maptiler#parameters)

Parameters


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Properties

Description

**Map Window**

The area of satellite data that will be rendered by the layer. Can be manipulated by drag & drop and MMB zooming.

**Latitude**

Allows you to specify a coordinate for the satellite data.

**Longitude**

Allows you to specify a coordinate for the satellite data.

**Zoom**

Controls the scale of the satellite data.

**Type**

Switches the render mode for the preview window.

**Preview Type**

Controls when the changes in the satellite position will be updated. If you're using a paid MapTiler plan this can make a difference in API requests.

**Flip X/Y**

Allows you to flip the satellite area.

**Create Sculpt Layer**

Converts the height data into a sculpt layer so you can further edit it.

**Height Resolution**

Specifies the resolution of the downloaded height data from MapTiler. Please note, that the resulting terrain detail of the Shape Layer is still dependant on your specified [level step](https://docs.world-creator.com/walkthrough/terrain-setup/level-step-system)
.

C**olor Resolution**

Specifies the resolution of the accompanying color map. The color map can be used in every material by enabling the "Use Shape Layer Color" toggle.

**Color Blending**

Controls the opacity of the color map.

**Saturation**

Lets you adjust the saturation of the satellite color.

**Contrast**

Lets you adjust the contrast of the satellite color.

**Brightness**

Lets you adjust the brightness of the satellite color.

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/shape-layers/maptiler#results)

Results


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

![](https://docs.world-creator.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2837684122-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FM6zsxw2jbMYEZbKqEwpa%252Fuploads%252FlLywEk29wHNxDqWLnuH9%252Fwalkthrough_shapelayers_maptiler_02.webp%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6020e813-2297-464b-8bd8-06ee39c20858&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=594268c8&sv=2)

![](https://docs.world-creator.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2837684122-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FM6zsxw2jbMYEZbKqEwpa%252Fuploads%252FqrOe66OqCOJJ7i9qcdKK%252Freference_shapelayers_maptiler_07.webp%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc6f8b237-2d1c-44d8-861c-e063d31b957f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7510a431&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/shape-layers/maptiler#setting-up-maptiler)

Setting up MapTiler


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The MapTiler Layer requires a service token from MapTiler to connect to their servers and download data in World Creator.

1

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/shape-layers/maptiler#create-a-maptiler-account)

Create a MapTiler Account

To obtain the service token, create an account at [https://www.maptiler.com/arrow-up-right](https://www.maptiler.com/)
. Either use a free account (with watermarks) or one of their paid account models.

2

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/shape-layers/maptiler#navigate-to-the-credentials-section)

Navigate to the Credentials section

After signing in, navigate to the **Account** settings and open the **Credentials** tab.

![](https://docs.world-creator.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2837684122-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FM6zsxw2jbMYEZbKqEwpa%252Fuploads%252FgvNlYnTZGxvl8l7vninA%252Freference_shapelayers_maptiler_01.webp%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D854be93b-3f23-41a3-bc41-3b4d0a243f34&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=dff1f0e8&sv=2)

3

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/shape-layers/maptiler#create-a-new-credential-for-world-creator)

Create a new credential for World Creator

Click the **New Credentials** button and enter a name. Then, click **Save**.

![](https://docs.world-creator.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2837684122-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FM6zsxw2jbMYEZbKqEwpa%252Fuploads%252FLiecfJBXlsFyRQYoNUwb%252Freference_shapelayers_maptiler_02.webp%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9e514004-a351-4c58-9d85-4cfe9b887958&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ab7a5f64&sv=2)

4

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/shape-layers/maptiler#copy-service-token)

Copy Service Token

![](https://docs.world-creator.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2837684122-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FM6zsxw2jbMYEZbKqEwpa%252Fuploads%252FmjEnaLGljoOX3yPttxTj%252Freference_shapelayers_maptiler_03.webp%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8713d48e-36ca-4ecf-a736-a65be9d5f2fe&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b2dd2109&sv=2)

5

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/shape-layers/maptiler#apply-token-in-wc)

Apply Token in WC

With your token navigate to the MapTiler Options tab and apply the token.

![](https://docs.world-creator.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2837684122-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FM6zsxw2jbMYEZbKqEwpa%252Fuploads%252FovqiQftmezRDRZEUoDyZ%252Freference_shapelayers_maptiler_04.webp%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D019d2536-2167-492c-8a7f-2f7222ca215f&width=300&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=adf16249&sv=2)

Last updated 6 months ago

Was this helpful?

*   [Overview](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/shape-layers/maptiler#overview)
    
*   [Video Guide](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/shape-layers/maptiler#video-guide)
    
*   [Parameters](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/shape-layers/maptiler#parameters)
    
*   [Results](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/shape-layers/maptiler#results)

# Materials | World Creator

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/biome/materials#overview)

Overview


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

World Creator offers an extensive toolset for texturing your terrain. Similar to filters, materials work in a bottom-up fashion and can be masked using the [Distribution System](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/distributions)
.

circle-info

To improve your material authoring experience it can be helpful to switch to the [Textured Render Mode](https://docs.world-creator.com/walkthrough/introduction/viewport-and-navigation)
. This disables sun lighting and renders the albedo of all materials directly without shading.

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/biome/materials#material-settings)

Material Settings


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Property

Description

**Tint**

Tints the material.

**Metalness**

Controls the metallic strength of the material.

**Roughness**

Controls the roughness of the material.

**Use Shape Layer Color**

Some Shape Layers (e.g. [MapTiler Layer](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/shape-layers/maptiler)
, [Stamp Layer](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/shape-layers/2d-stamp)
) carry their own supplemental albedo information. If this option is enabled, the material will display the combined shape layer color data as its color information.

**Enable Emission**

This enables the Emissive Strength slider for this material, creating a luminescent material.

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/biome/materials#texturing-settings)

Texturing Settings


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Property

Description

**Texture Type**

This allows you to switch between all the different texture types. It enables you to link textures in various arrangements to the material.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/biome/materials#texture-type-none)

Texture Type - None

This is the most basic type of material, which uses the **Tint Color** provided in the material settings for colouring. No other texture detail is used.

Showcase

Guide by Design with TP

![](https://docs.world-creator.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2837684122-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FM6zsxw2jbMYEZbKqEwpa%252Fuploads%252FkpdExQZCDW7k65INdpQU%252Freference_materials_color_01.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd5d142b4-830f-4712-8b76-553b777fc44c&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=add19985&sv=2)

Colored Terrain

![](https://docs.world-creator.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2837684122-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FM6zsxw2jbMYEZbKqEwpa%252Fuploads%252FnzYWoZCWfDPFUlhEvkXB%252Freference_materials_color_02.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D034527e2-bca6-4fdf-beb5-81237040823e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=24bb61fa&sv=2)

Blue color Material masked by Fluid Simulation

This video shows basic color materials. It demonstrates the functionality in WC 2024.3; the UI has since been adjusted slightly, but the functionality remains the same.

Intro to Color Materials by Design with TP

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/biome/materials#texture-type-set-package)

Texture Type - Set / Package

The 'Texture Type - Set' option allows you to assign textures individually to the standard PBR shader. It can automatically import multiple textures for a material based on their names (e.g. 'Grass\_Color', 'Grass\_Normal', and so on).

The Texture Type - Package works similarly, though it uses a ZIP file containing all the textures. This makes it easy to apply materials with one click.

Showcase

World Creator Guide

Guide by Design with TP

![](https://docs.world-creator.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2837684122-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FM6zsxw2jbMYEZbKqEwpa%252Fuploads%252FaKdUHoRmXL5gpVaHKTqQ%252Freference_materials_texture_01.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbd6ff905-0175-4820-905e-b7f13ad44cd9&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=35a957cd&sv=2)

Using a Texture

![](https://docs.world-creator.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2837684122-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FM6zsxw2jbMYEZbKqEwpa%252Fuploads%252FDnuSOEcFoNHcgdzpFTPz%252Freference_materials_texture_02.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbe63d3b9-2c4f-4e21-8826-e5805b18e959&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b79d71c8&sv=2)

This video shows the function of the Set Texture Type. It demonstrates the functionality in WC 2024.3; the UI has since been adjusted slightly, but the functionality remains the same.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/biome/materials#texture-type-substance)

Texture Type - Substance

This allows you to load Substance materials. The properties exposed in the Substance UI are displayed in WC and can be adjusted to tweak the exposed material parameters using the Substance Engine.

Modified Substance Parameters

This video shows the function of the Substance Texture type. This video demonstrates the functionality in WC 2024.3; the UI has since been adjusted slightly, but the functionality remains the same.

Intro to Substance Materials by Design with TP

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/biome/materials#shared-parameters)

Shared Parameters

These parameters are available for all texture types except 'None'.

Property

Description

**Saturation**

Alters the saturation of the albedo texture.

**Contrast**

Alters the contrast of the albedo texture.

**Brightness**

Alters the brightness of the albedo texture.

**Normal Strength**

Changes the strength of the normal texture.

**Flip Normal Y**

Flips the up channel of the normal map. Some rendering engines have inverted Y channels for normal maps, this allows you to load in all kinds of normal maps.

**Is Gloss**

Switches the roughness map to be interpreted as a gloss map.

**Tile Size**

Adjusts the tile size of the final material.

**Tile Offset X/Y**

Shifts the texture in the X/Y direction.

**Triplanar Projection**

Applies triplanar projection to the material. This means that the texture is not only projected from the top down as usual, but is also projected from the X, Y and Z axes and then blended together. This results in a material that is able to add detail to steep surfaces that would normally be problematic due to stretched UVs. _Triplanar Projection is a shader-based effect that cannot be exported as a texture. To get the same effect in your preferred rendering engine, look for a triplanar shader in their respective material system._

**Stochastic Distribution**

Switches the standard tile based sampling to a randomized sampler that reduces visible tiling over large areas. _The Stochastic Distribution is a shader-based effect that can be exported in a baked colour map of the terrain. However, if you plan to use tiled textures (which is highly recommended for close up detailed terrain), you'll need to look for a similar shading effect in your render engine._

**Height Blending**

Applies height blending to the material. This works in conjunction with a displacement texture.

**Displacement Enabled**

Enables displacement for the material.

**Height Scale**

Adjusts the height of the displacement.

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/biome/materials#gradient-settings)

Gradient Settings


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Gradients can be added to every material in World Creator. This can be used to further enhance base materials or texture details with procedurally generated, terrain-adjusted gradient colouring. When you use the gradient features, a second distribution stack (**Gradient Distribution**) becomes available, where you can create the base gradient used for colour application.

Showcase

Guide by Design with TP

![](https://docs.world-creator.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2837684122-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FM6zsxw2jbMYEZbKqEwpa%252Fuploads%252FJKBGibZGQd1D9BZJB2bm%252Freference_materials_gradient_01.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D336adb0b-d61d-4a47-aeaf-a81e76b251e4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5a307661&sv=2)

Gradient Material

![](https://docs.world-creator.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2837684122-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FM6zsxw2jbMYEZbKqEwpa%252Fuploads%252FEwDjEfn7R5PjlJ1yLL97%252Freference_materials_gradient_02.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9755d082-10de-48ce-8960-5b9c51efb59a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=71008f41&sv=2)

Terrain Gradient

![](https://docs.world-creator.com/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2837684122-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FM6zsxw2jbMYEZbKqEwpa%252Fuploads%252FC4aYnFTIzI6cxREbXcVO%252Freference_materials_gradient_03.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5ef19583-da8b-483c-94f2-e2a7b9ad747d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c5766d7b&sv=2)

Close Up

In WC 2025.1, the materials have been overhauled so that gradients can now be applied to every material. This tutorial explains the general concepts of how gradients work.

Guide by Design with TP

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/biome/materials#parameters)

Parameters

Properties

Description

**Gradient Enabled**

Enables the gradient settings for this material.

**Gradient Panel**

Allows you to build your gradient. The gradient is mapped left to right (between the lower to indicators) to the black to white gradient produced by the Gradient Distribution specified in the material.

**Invert Gradient**

Inverts the sampling direction of the Gradient Distribution stack.

**Saturation**

Alters the saturation of the resulting gradient material.

**Contrast**

Alters the contrast of the resulting gradient material.

**Brightness**

Alters the brightness of the resulting gradient material.

**Gradient Detail**

Adds additional noise to the gradient to increase the detail of the resulting color map.

**Seed**

The Seed of the Gradient Detail noise.

**Detail Strength**

Controls the impact the details have on the source gradient.

**Detail Probability**

Adjust the amount of details added to the gradient.

**Shading Strength**

Defines the strength of the change of brightness in the details.

**Offset Strength**

Defines the similarity of the details to neighboring colors. A large offset strength means that the detail contains similarities to colors further away while a small value means that the details stick to the neighboring colors.

Last updated 6 months ago

# 반복 값 | World Creator

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/ko/reference/terrain/effects/repeat-value#undefined)

개요


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Repeat Value 효과는 주어진 값에 모듈로 연산을 적용하여 반복 패턴을 생성합니다. 예를 들어 레이어링 효과를 만드는 데 사용할 수 있습니다.

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/ko/reference/terrain/effects/repeat-value#undefined-1)

매개변수


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

속성

설명

**반복 횟수**

0-1 범위에서 적용되는 반복 횟수입니다.

**미러**

더 부드러운 레이어를 만들기 위해 두 번째 반복마다 값을 반전합니다.

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/ko/reference/terrain/effects/repeat-value#undefined-2)

# Sculpt | World Creator

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/shape-layers/sculpt#overview)

Overview


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Sculpt Layers enable you to design a terrain from scratch or modify an existing terrain you created procedurally to fit your requirements. As the name suggests, sculpt layers enable you to sculpt the terrain. You can use your mouse and keyboard, but it is recommended to employ a graphics tablet, such as the Wacom Cintiq Pro (World Creator also supports other graphics tablets).

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/shape-layers/sculpt#video-guides)

Video Guides


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

World Creator Guide

Guide by Design with TP

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/shape-layers/sculpt#layer-parameters)

Layer Parameters


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/shape-layers/sculpt#sculpt-settings)

Sculpt Settings

Allows you to import/export and edit the sculpt layer.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/shape-layers/sculpt#layer-settings)

Layer Settings

Properties

Description

**Resolution**

Allows you to set the resolution of the sculpt layer, increase this to sculpt with finer detail.

B**ase Shape Preview**

Stops World Creator from applying its filters while moving the area or sculpting the terrain. This improves the performance on GPUs with lower specifications.

circle-info

Usually a resolution 32x32px is enough since you most of the time want shape layers to operate on the lower level steps so that World Creators filter stack has enough levels to operate on.

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/shape-layers/sculpt#editing-parameters)

Editing Parameters


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/shape-layers/sculpt#brush-tools)

Brush Tools

Classical brush tools like in other applications. Choose your preferred tool by clicking on it, and then draw with your mouse (press the left mouse button on the terrain). The following functions are available:

Properties

Description

**Raise**

Adds material to the terrain.

**Lower**

Removes material from the terrain.

**Smooth**

Averages the height under the brush.

**Flatten**

Flattens the terrain according to the **Flatten Height** in the parameters below.

**Rotate**

Lets you rotate the terrain in your brush radius around your clicked point.

**Scale**

Scales the terrain in your brush radius from the point where you clicked

**Tilt**

Tilts the brush area towards the mouse. Move the mouse outwards to increase the slope.

**Push/Pull**

Allows you to drag & drop the terrain up/down.

**Align**

Flattens the terrain according to the point where you clicked.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/shape-layers/sculpt#grid-tools)

Grid Tools

World Creator has grid tools to improve performance and provide new possibilities and functions. The concept involves manipulating terrain using an underlying grid. The workflow entails selecting grid cells using a brush and then manipulating them accordingly.

Properties

Description

**Add**

Raises or lowers the terrain.

**Align**

Flattens the terrain to the height your cursor was at when you clicked.

**Duplicate**

Allows you to copy your selected area to another spot on the terrain.

**Rotate**

Rotates the selected area along your mouse direction.

**Scale**

Scales the selected area according to your mouse distance.

**Tilt**

Tilts your selection in the direction you moved your mouse after clicking. Move the mouse outwards to increase the slope.

**Pull**

Raises the selected area.

**Push**

Lowers the selected area.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/shape-layers/sculpt#actions)

Actions

The operations are utilized to rapidly implement precise modifications. Please refer to the list below to understand the function of each operation.

Properties

Description

**Flip X**

Flips the terrain along the X axis.

**Flip Y**

Flips the terrain along the Y axis.

**Rot Left**

Rotates the terrain by 90°.

**Rot Right**

Rotates the terrain by 90°.

**Flatten**

Flattens the whole terrain.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/shape-layers/sculpt#universal)

Universal

Properties

Description

**Operation Mode**

Allows you to restrict modifications only to happen additive or subtractive.

**Falloff Mode**

Offers different brush falloff modes.

**Radius**

The radius of the brush.

**Smooth**

The size of the brush smoothing.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/reference/terrain/shape-layers/sculpt#brush-settings)

Brush Settings

Properties

Description

**Brush**

Allows you to specify several preinstalled brushes as well as import your own custom brushes.

**Strength**

Controls the strength of the current selected brush.

**Height Change**

How much height is added/subtracted by the brush.

**Flatten Height**

The target height for the flatten.

**Rotation**

Rotates the brush pattern.

**Random Rotation**

Adds random rotation to the brush pattern.

**Align to Draw Direction**

Orients the brush pattern to the drawing direction.

Last updated 6 months ago

# 번짐 | World Creator

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/ko/reference/terrain/effects/smear#undefined)

개요


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Smear 효과는 분포 위를 흐르는 물 입자가 아래쪽으로 침식을 일으키는 것을 시뮬레이트합니다. 이는 다른 응용 프로그램에서 알려진 Fluvial Advection 및 Color Erosion과 유사합니다. 세척된 퇴적 효과를 생성하기 위해 그라디언트 재료와 함께 사용하도록 설계되었습니다.

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/ko/reference/terrain/effects/smear#undefined-1)

매개변수


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

속성

설명

**각도 무작위성**

다음에 추가적인 무작위성을 추가합니다 **스폰 각도 범위.**

**무작위 확률**

입자가 생성될 확률입니다.

**스폰 각도 범위**

입자가 생성될 경사 각도입니다.

**업데이트 간격**

시뮬레이션 단계 업데이트의 빈도를 제어합니다.

**반복**

시뮬레이션 반복 횟수입니다.

**스텝 크기**

각 업데이트마다 입자가 이동하는 거리를 제어합니다.

**관성**

이동 중 지형 변화에 대해 입자가 얼마나 빨리 반응하는지 제어합니다.

**타입**

운반된 값이 마스크에 어떻게 기록될지 지정합니다.

**정리 단계**

입자가 안정된 후 추가 정리 시뮬레이션 단계를 적용합니다.

[hashtag](https://docs.world-creator.com/ko/reference/terrain/effects/smear#undefined-2)

------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
